<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡只是簡單的很粗略的說明地獄當中的苦具，不是說在這些大地獄中，沒有其他令有情受苦的器具，苦具很多種，但是無法完全說出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、近邊那落迦2　午一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科近邊那落迦，說明近大地獄旁邊的地獄受苦的情形，分二科；第一科標，標出受用治罰重苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於近邊諸那落迦中，有情之類受用如是治罰重苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又靠近大地獄旁邊有很多近邊地獄，那裏的有情會受用如下文所說的對治處罰的極重苦受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋3　未一、總標四園</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科總標四園，總相標出八大地獄每一個地獄旁邊還有四個園。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂彼一切諸大那落迦皆有四方、四岸、四門，鐵牆圍繞。從其四方四門出已，其一一門外有四出園。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又每一個大地獄都有四個方向，四個邊，四個門，由鐵牆圍繞。從四方四門出去，每一個門外面有四個出園。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、別顯其相2　申一、辨苦緣4　酉一、煻煨齊膝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別顯其相，各別說明這四園的相狀，分二科；第一科辨苦緣，說明這四園受苦的緣，又分四科；第一科煻煨齊膝，受煻煨齊膝苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂煻煨齊膝。彼諸有情出求舍宅，遊行至此。下足之時，皮肉及血，并即銷爛，舉足還生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四園受四種苦，第一種是煻煨齊膝苦。煻煨指熱的灰火，這熱的灰火的高度像人的膝蓋一樣高。獄中的有情出大地獄四個門後，就想找個房舍屋宅休息，走到此地來，腳踏下去的時候，皮肉跟血就一齊銷爛，可是腳一提起來又復原了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、死尸糞泥2　戌一、遊行陷沒苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科死尸糞泥，受死尸糞泥苦，分二科；第一科遊行陷沒苦，受遊行陷沒苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p290"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次此煻煨無間，即有死尸糞泥。此諸有情為求舍宅，從彼出已，漸漸遊行，陷入其中，首足俱沒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種是死尸糞泥苦。獄中有情過了煻煨無間這一關後，接著要往前時，又有屍體、糞便、淤泥。為求另外一個比較好的房舍屋宅，所以從這種煻煨齊膝地方出來，漸漸遊行，到了這死尸糞泥的地方時就全部掉下去，頭跟腳都淹沒在死尸糞泥中，這是很臭的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、諸蟲唼食苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科諸蟲唼食苦，受諸蟲唼食苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又尸糞泥內多有諸蟲，名孃矩吒，穿皮入肉，斷筋破骨，取髓而食。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　掉到尸糞泥去時裏面有很多蟲，這些蟲稱為孃矩吒，據說這種蟲身長一尺，身體是白的，頭是黑的，可以穿破人的皮爬到肉裡面，將有情的筋咬斷骨頭啃破，取有情的骨髓來吃。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、刀劍刃路等3　戌一、刀劍刃路</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科刀劍刃路等，受刀劍刃路等苦，分三科；第一科刀劍刃路，刃，也是刀，像刀子一樣的道路。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次尸糞泥無間，有利刀劍仰刃為路。彼諸有情為求舍宅，從彼出已，遊行至此。下足之時，皮肉筋血悉皆銷爛，舉足之時，還復如故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三受刀劍刃路等苦。尸糞泥過了以後，沒有間斷的，有很鋒利的刀劍、劍尖向上的道路。獄中的眾有情為了找個房舍屋宅休息，從尸糞泥出來以後，遊行到此處。腳踏下去時，皮肉筋血全部被刀子銷爛，等到腳舉起來時，又恢復原狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、刃葉林2　亥一、刃葉斫截苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科刃葉林，受刃葉林苦，分二科；第一科刃葉斫截苦，受刃葉斫截苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次刀劍刃路無間，有刃葉林。彼諸有情為求舍宅，從彼出已，往趣彼蔭。纔坐其下，微風遂起，刃葉墮落，斫截其身一切支節，便即躄地。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過了刀劍刃路之後，有樹葉像刀子一樣的地方。獄中的眾有情為了找個舍宅休息，從刀劍刃路出來以後，看到樹就很高興，走到樹蔭下面。才坐在樹底下，就吹起一陣風，刃葉紛紛飄落下來，砍殺有情身中一切支節，有情的手腳被刀葉砍斷掉下來就昏倒在地。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、黑狗噉食苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科黑狗噉食苦，受黑狗噉食苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有黑釐狗，摣掣脊𦛗而噉食之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種很貪心的狗稱為黑釐狗，將有情身體的脊骨拉扯開來吃掉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、鐵設拉末梨林2　亥一、刺鋒貫身</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科鐵設拉末梨林，受鐵設拉末梨林苦，分二科；第一科刺鋒貫身，受刺鋒貫身苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p291"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從此刃葉林無間，有鐵設拉末梨林。彼諸有情為求舍宅，便來趣之，遂登其上。當登之時，一切刺鋒悉迴向下，欲下之時，一切刺鋒復迴向上。由此因緣，貫刺其身，遍諸支節。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從刃葉林緊接著，有鐵設拉末梨林，長多刺的樹林。獄中的眾有情為了追求另外一個比較好的舍宅，就來到這種樹林，登上鐵設拉末梨林。當要往上走時，一切刀鋒全部往下刺他，當有情要往下走時，一切刀鋒就迴轉向上刺有情。由於這種因緣，身體上下都有刀子貫刺著，手腳所有支節通通被刀子所刺殺。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、大烏啄眼</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科大烏啄眼，鳥來吃眼睛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">爾時便有鐵觜大烏上彼頭上，或上其髆，探啄眼睛而噉食之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這時就有鐵觜大鳥飛到有情的頭上，或胳膊上，探啄有情的眼睛吞噉而食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、廣大灰河3　戌一、墮入煎煮苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科廣大灰河，受廣大灰河苦，分三科；第一科墮入煎煮苦，受墮入煎煮苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從鐵設拉末梨林無間，有廣大河，沸熱灰水彌滿其中。彼諸有情尋求舍宅，從彼出已，來墮此中。猶如以豆置之大鑊，然猛熾火而煎煮之，隨湯騰涌，周旋迴復。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四是廣大灰河苦。從鐵設拉末梨林出來時，有廣大的河，裏面有滾熱的灰水彌滿其中。獄中的眾有情為了追求另外一個比較好的舍宅，從鐵設拉末梨林出來以後，來到這個地方。好像以豆子放在大鍋子裏面，有很猛烈熾盛的火而煎煮著有情，有情就隨著湯水沸騰翻滾，來回旋轉不停。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、獄卒遮障苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科獄卒遮障苦，受獄卒遮障苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於河兩岸有諸獄卒，手執杖索及以大網，行列而住，遮彼有情，不令得出，或以索羂，或以網漉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　接著往前走，在河的兩岸還有獄卒，有情想要出來，但獄卒手拿木杖、繩索及大網，行行排列站在旁邊，遮止有情，使有情不能從灰河出來，或用繩子將有情綁住，或用網子將有情撈出來又放回去煎煮，受獄卒遮障苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、饑渴所須苦2　亥一、問欲所須</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科饑渴所須苦，受饑渴所須苦，這時就很飢渴了，分二科；第一科問欲所須，問地獄有情何所須求？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復置廣大熱鐵地上，仰彼有情而問之言：汝等今者欲何所須？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又將有情放在大熱鐵上，將有情臉朝上問說：你們現在需要什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p292"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、隨答治罰2　天一、鐵丸置口</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨答治罰，隨著有情的回答來治罰他們，分二科；第一科鐵丸置口，受鐵丸置口苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是答言：我等今者竟無覺知，然為種種饑苦所逼。時彼獄卒即以鐵鉗鉗口令開，便以極熱燒然鐵丸置其口中，餘如前說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果這些罪人回答說：我們現在也不知道什麼事情，可是我們現在很飢餓很苦，為種種饑苦所逼迫！獄卒聽到就用鐵鉗將他們的口打開，用很熱的鐵丸放到他們的口中，其他的如前所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、洋銅灌口</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科洋銅灌口，受洋銅灌口苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼答言：我今唯為渴苦所逼。爾時獄卒便即洋銅以灌其口。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果有情回答說：我們現在只是為口渴的苦所逼迫。這時獄卒就拿燒熱的洋銅灌到有情的口裏。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、明邊際</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明邊際，說明受苦的邊際。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由是因緣，長時受苦，乃至先世所造一切能感那落迦惡不善業未盡未出。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於這種因緣，長時間受苦，乃至過去生所造的惡業，業力還沒有完全受盡，還不能出離這個地方以前，都一直要受這種苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、結成四數</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結成四數，結說有四個園。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中若刀劍刃路、若刃葉林、若鐵設拉末梨林總之為一，故有四園。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這當中煻煨齊膝是第一種園，死屍糞泥是第二種園，刀劍刃路等是第三種園，廣大灰河是第四種園，全部都在一個門外面，因此有四園。東西南北各有一門，每一個門外都有四種園，稱為近邊地獄。所以每一個大地獄旁邊有十六個近邊地獄，近邊地獄也稱為遊增地獄，八個大地獄旁邊共有一百二十八個遊增地獄。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、八寒那落迦2　午一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科八寒那落迦，說明八種寒冰地獄的苦，分二科；第一科標，標出受極重寒苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於寒那落迦受生有情，多受如是極重寒苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又在寒冰地獄受生的有情，多分受如下所說極重寒冷的痛苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋6　未一、皰那落迦2　申一、辨相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分六科；第一科皰那落迦，皰（音泡），像面皰一樣的地獄，受皰那落迦苦，又分二科；第一科辨相，說明苦的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p293"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂皰那落迦中受生有情，即為彼地極重廣大寒觸所觸，一切身分悉皆卷縮，猶如瘡皰。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在皰那落迦中受生的有情，因為該地獄中有非常廣大的很強烈的寒冷所接觸，全身都卷縮成小小的瘡皰一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、結名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結名，結說名皰那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">故此那落迦名皰那落迦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此這種地獄稱為皰那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、皰裂那落迦3　申一、標差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科皰裂那落迦，如膿皰裂開來的地獄，分三科；第一科標差別，標出與皰那落迦不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">皰裂那落迦與此差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　皰裂那落迦與皰那落迦又有差別，痛苦更大。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋彼相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋彼相，解釋皰裂那落迦的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">猶如皰潰，膿血流出，其瘡卷皺。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　皰裂那落迦就像膿皰已經潰爛了，膿血流出來，冷到連瘡都卷縮起來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、結得名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結得名，結得名皰裂那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">故此那落迦名為皰裂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此這種地獄稱為皰裂那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、喝哳詀等三那落迦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科喝哳詀等三那落迦，說明喝哳詀等三種那落迦的苦受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又喝哳詀、郝郝凡、虎虎凡，此三那落迦由彼有情苦音差別以立其名。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又喝哳詀、郝郝凡、虎虎凡，這三種寒冰地獄，由於太冷，冷到發出來的苦聲有差別而安立不同的名稱。第一種差別稱為喝哳詀，是指冷到嘴唇不能動，只有舌頭能動，顫抖著舌頭發出來的聲音。郝郝凡，是舌頭不能動只有嘴唇能動，因寒冷的哭聲而得名。虎虎凡，是冷到嘴唇跟舌頭都不能動，只有喉頭內的震氣，那種喘氣的聲音，稱為虎虎凡。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、青蓮那落迦2　申一、辨相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科青蓮那落迦，是指地獄有情的皮膚因為被寒冰所割像蓮花一樣，分二科；第一科辨相，說明受苦的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p294"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">青蓮那落迦中，由彼地極重廣大寒觸所觸，一切身分悉皆青瘀，皮膚破裂，或五或六。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　青蓮地獄中，由於那個地方有極重、極廣大、強烈寒冷的觸所觸，有情全身各部分都變成青瘀，而且皮膚破裂成五個部分或六個部分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、結名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結名，結得名青蓮那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">故此那落迦名曰青蓮。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此這種地獄稱為青蓮那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、紅蓮那落迦3　申一、標差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科紅蓮那落迦，這是第七種寒冰地獄，分三科；第一科標差別，標出與青蓮那落迦不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">紅蓮那落迦與此差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　紅蓮那落迦地獄與此青蓮那落迦有所差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋彼相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋彼相，說明紅蓮那落迦的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">過此青已，色變紅赤，皮膚分裂或十或多。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過了青蓮那落迦以後，到紅蓮那落迦時被寒冰破壞得更嚴重，皮膚從青色變成紅赤，因為冷得太過，皮膚分裂成十個部分或更多，他的肉好像紅蓮花一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、結得名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結得名，結名紅蓮那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">故此那落迦名曰紅蓮。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此這種地獄稱為紅蓮那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未六、大紅蓮那落迦3　申一、標差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科大紅蓮那落迦，這是第八種寒冰地獄，分三科；第一科標差別，標出與紅蓮那落迦不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大紅蓮那落迦與此差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大紅蓮地獄與紅蓮那落迦又更不一樣了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋彼相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋彼相，解釋大紅蓮那落迦的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂彼身分極大紅赤，皮膚分裂或百或多。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為更冷所以身體更紅了，皮膚分裂成一百個部分或更多。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p295"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、結得名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結得名，結名大紅蓮那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">故此那落迦名大紅蓮。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此這種地獄稱為大紅蓮那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、獨一那落迦3　午一、標因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科獨一那落迦，就是孤獨地獄，以上所說八寒地獄或八大地獄，有的說八熱地獄，是眾生的共業增上所感，有很多人一起在裏面受苦，現在獨一那落迦，就是只有一個人在那裏受苦，因此稱為獨一那落迦，分三科；第一科標因，標出生獨一那落迦的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又獨一那落迦中受生有情，各於自身自業所感，多受如是種種大苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又獨一大地獄中受生的有情，是由自身自己造業所感的業報，多受如前所說的種種大苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、指說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科指說，指如《采菉豆子經》中廣說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如吉祥問采菉豆子經中廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如《吉祥問采菉豆子經》中說了很多有關地獄的事。孤獨地獄處所不一定，有時候在江邊，有時候在河邊，有情可能掉到江裏河裏，或山邊或是曠野無人居住的地方，或是在地下，或在其他的地方，一個人在那裡死掉，一個人在那裡受地獄的痛苦。孤獨地獄有很多到處都有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、結名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結名，結名獨一那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">故此那落迦名為獨一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此這種地獄稱為獨一那落迦，就是一個人在那裏受苦的那落迦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是說到獨一那落迦。前面說了：寒那落迦、近邊那落迦、獨一那落迦、大那落迦，總共有四種地獄；若說寒那落迦有八種，大那落迦也有八種，合說有十八地獄。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、傍生有情2　巳一、相殘害苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科傍生有情，說明畜生的情況，分二科；第一科相殘害苦，互相殘害的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又傍生趣更相殘害，如羸弱者為諸彊力之所殺害，由此因緣受種種苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又傍生就是畜生，因為牠們的身體多分都是橫的，也有少分向旁邊走，像螃蟹，又種類很多而且很愚癡，所以稱為傍生。牠們互相殺害，如果力量小的就被力量大的殺害，比方說貓捉老鼠，老虎會殺害鹿，或者大的吃小，由此因緣有種種痛苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、不自在苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不自在苦，受不自在苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">以不自在，他所驅馳，多被鞭撻，與彼人天為資生具。由此因緣具受種種極重苦惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為不自在，被他人所驅趕，而且多半被人鞭打，通常都是作為人與天的食物，所以說與彼人天為資助生活的資具。由於這種因緣牠們受到種種非常重的苦惱。牠們為什麼生到畜生來呢？ 在《業報差別經》及《六道伽陀經》裏有詳細說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p296"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、餓鬼有情3　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科餓鬼有情，說明餓鬼有情所受苦，分三科；第一科標，標出三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又餓鬼趣略有三種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又餓鬼道要略而言有三種有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列舉出三種餓鬼有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、由外障礙飲食，二者、由內障礙飲食，三者、飲食無有障礙。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一由外障礙受用飲食，第二由內身障礙受用飲食，第三飲食沒有障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋3　午一、由外障礙飲食3　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科由外障礙飲食，由於受到外在的環境障礙受用飲食，又分三科；第一科徵，問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何由外障礙飲食？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是由外面障礙受用飲食？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋3　申一、出業因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科出業因，說出業因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂彼有情由習上品慳故，生鬼趣中，常與饑渴相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類有情由於熏習上品慳貪，本身有條件有財物可以解決他人的苦難，可是不肯做，所以生到鬼趣中，常與饑渴相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、顯彼相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯彼相，說明受報的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">皮肉血脈皆悉枯槁，猶如火炭，頭髮髼亂，其面黯黑，唇口乾焦，常以其舌舐略口面。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類餓鬼因為沒有東西吃，所以皮肉和血脈都很乾枯，好像火炭一樣，頭髮蓬鬆散亂，顏面黯黑，嘴唇與嘴巴很乾燥像燒焦一樣，常常伸出舌頭用口水來舔自己的臉和口。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、辨苦緣2　酉一、慞惶馳走苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨苦緣，說明種種痛苦的因緣，分二科；第一科慞惶馳走苦，很恐怖走得很快的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">饑渴慞惶，處處馳走。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為很飢餓內心很恐怖，所以到處奔走想要討得食物。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p297"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、不得泉池苦2　戌一、由他障</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不得泉池苦，受不得泉池苦，分二科；第一科由他障，由其他有情障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所到泉池，為餘有情手執刀杖及以羂索行列守護，令不得趣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所到的泉池，有其他的有情拿著刀杖或繩子排排站在旁邊守護、擋著，使餓鬼無法喝泉裡的水。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、由自障</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由自障，由自身障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或彊趣之，便見其泉變成膿血，自不欲飲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果勉強衝進去，一看，泉水都變成膿血，於是自己又不想喝了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等鬼，是名由外障礙飲食。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類的鬼，稱為由外障礙飲食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、由內障礙飲食3　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由內障礙飲食，本身有障礙不能吃東西，分三科；第一科徵，先問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何由內障礙飲食？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是由內障礙飲食？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂彼有情，口或如針，口或如炬，或復頸癭，其腹寬大。由此因緣，縱得飲食，無他障礙，自然不能若噉若飲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由內障礙飲食的餓鬼，口像針孔那麼小，或者是像火炬會噴出猛火，或脖子長瘤，或者是肚子很大。由於這種因緣，就算拿到食物沒有他人來障礙他，但任何東西到嘴巴或吞不下去、或噴出猛火將東西燒成灰，自然無法吃喝。這是很苦的，由自己本身障礙自己不能吃也不能喝。可見慳吝的果報很可怕。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等鬼，是名由內障礙飲食。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類的鬼，稱為由內障礙飲食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p298"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、飲食無有障礙3　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科飲食無有障礙，飲食沒有障礙的情況，分三科；第一科徵，先問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何飲食無有障礙？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是飲食沒有障礙？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋3　申一、飲噉燒燃苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科飲噉燒燃苦，受飲噉燒燃苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有餓鬼，名猛焰鬘。隨所飲噉，皆被燒然。由此因緣，饑渴大苦未嘗暫息。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　飲食沒有障礙，是指有飲食可是無法吃下去。這類餓鬼，稱為猛焰鬘，猛焰，是指猛火，猛火結成的花蔓。隨他所吃的東西，都被口裡噴出的火燒掉了，由於這種因緣一直很餓很渴，這種又餓又渴的大苦，從來沒有停過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、唯食糞穢苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科唯食糞穢苦，只有吃糞穢的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有餓鬼，名食糞穢。或有一分食糞飲溺；或有一分唯能飲噉極可厭惡生熟臭穢，縱得香美而不能食。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有餓鬼，專門在有糞穢的地方住，名為食糞穢。這種食糞鬼吃糞喝尿，吃的是不淨物；或有一分食糞是鬼只能吃令人極為厭惡、極為臭穢的生或熟的食品，即使得到味道很香很美好的食物也不能吃。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、唯噉自肉苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科唯噉自肉苦，只有吃自己身肉的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有一分自割身肉而噉食之，縱得餘食，竟不能噉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或有一種餓鬼將自己身上的肉割下來吃，即使得到其他的食物，也不能吃。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結名飲食無有障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等鬼，是名飲食無有障礙。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此這類的鬼，名為飲食沒有障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、人趣有情2　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科人趣有情，說明人趣有情所受的苦，分二科；第一科標，標出受匱乏之苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又人趣中受生有情，多受如是匱乏之苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又在人趣受生的有情，多分受用如下文所說的有所缺乏的痛苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p299"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、列2　午一、匱乏苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出匱乏之苦，分二科；第一科匱乏苦，受各種匱乏苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所謂俱生饑渴匱乏苦；所欲不果匱乏苦；麤疏飲食匱乏苦；逼切追求攝受等匱乏苦；時節變異，若寒若熱匱乏苦；無有舍宅覆障，所作淋漏匱乏苦；黑闇等障，所作事業皆悉休廢匱乏苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在人趣中受生的有情多受七種苦：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、俱生饑渴匱乏苦，人趣有情多受與生俱來果報所招感的饑渴匱乏苦。　二、所欲不果匱乏苦，所歡喜的事情都不能滿足，是一種求不得苦。想要的東西常常得不到，希望自己各方面都很好可是也達不到，種種的所欲不果匱乏之苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、麤疏飲食匱乏苦，吃的食品很粗糙的匱乏苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、逼切追求攝受等匱乏苦，受他人的逼迫打罵、追求食物、名利、事業、攝受其他有情等匱乏苦。例如每個人從小到大都有被老師被父母逼切的苦，追求食物、名利、事業，總是追求不到最圓滿的，想將所追求的有情或財物等取過來受用，也不一定能夠滿願。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、時節變異，若寒若熱匱乏苦，春夏秋冬，冷的時候衣服不夠穿很苦，熱的時候沒有避暑的地方或冷氣不冷也很苦，冷時也苦熱時也苦，所以冷熱也是種種的苦。《雲棲法彙》卷18說人是：「畏寒時欲夏，苦熱復思冬」，唯有「妄想能消滅，安身處處同。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、無有舍宅覆障，所作淋漏匱乏苦，沒房舍屋宅遮覆障住風雨，於做事時受風吹雨打等種種匱乏苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、黑闇等障，所作事業皆悉休廢匱乏苦。如果沒有光明，所從事的事業都要受停止廢棄的匱乏苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　人有各式各樣的苦，當然不是每個人都有這種苦，但俱生饑渴匱乏苦是每個人都有的，其他就看個人的業報而有差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《六道伽陀經》說，如果不偷盜也不布施，不慳吝也不貪，決定得到人身，但衣食多辛苦；如果不偷盜也不貪瞋，能夠守分安住，以美味供養聖賢三寶，生到人界，壽命具足，而且顏色光彩，諸事吉祥也沒有病。如果常做施食的工作，對三寶有淨信又具足慚愧，這種人就會有富貴端嚴，廣饒資蓄等。總之如果有布施就沒有這些匱乏苦，如果沒有布施就有如上所說種種的匱乏之苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、老病死苦2　未一、顯自趣有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科老病死苦，做人也有各式各樣的老病死，分二科；第一科顯自趣有，顯示人趣有這種苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又受變壞老病死苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又領受五蘊種種的變壞、衰老、生病、死亡的痛苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、簡那落迦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡那落迦，簡除地獄有情沒有死苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由那落迦中謂死為樂，故於彼趣不立為苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　地獄的眾生沒有死苦，為什麼呢？因為假如真的能死是件快樂的事，就不用在地獄中繼續受苦，可能生到畜生、餓鬼或人，可以往上一層，所以死對地獄的人來說是一件好事。因為常常不能死，前面說活了又死、死了又活，等活地獄這樣，一直到罪報受完才能夠死，所以地獄沒有死苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又受變壞老病死苦等者：此中死苦唯除那落迦，餘一切趣皆應建立。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　死苦，只有地獄的人沒有死苦，因為死對這類眾生來說是好事，其他人、天、畜生、餓鬼諸趣都有死苦，但那落迦沒有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、天趣有情2　巳一、欲界諸天2　午一、釋3　未一、死墮苦3　申一、標簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科天趣有情，說明天趣有情所受的苦，分二科；第一科欲界諸天，說明欲界天有情所受苦，又分二科；第一科釋，先解釋，又分三科；第一科死墮苦，欲界天的人有死墮苦，又分三科；第一科標簡，標示簡別出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又天趣中無解支節苦，而有死墮苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又天趣中天人修十善業，沒有解支節苦，可是死了會墮到欲界或地獄、餓鬼、畜生受生，前生的業力現前，所以有死墮苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又天趣中無解支節苦者：此解支節，如前意地中說：除天、那落迦，所餘生處一切皆有。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/01.htm#2963:646">陵本一卷十五頁十七行77</a>）應準彼釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　解支節苦，如前〈意地〉卷1，37頁所說：除了天人及地獄，其餘生處都有。如本論卷1所說應當準照那裡所說解釋這段文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p300"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、引說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科引說，引經中所說為證。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如經中說：有諸天子將欲沒時，五相先現。一、衣無垢染，有垢染現；二、鬘舊不萎，今乃萎顇；三、兩腋汗流；四、身便臭穢；五、天及天子不樂本座。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如經中說：有些欲界天子將死時，有五衰相會出現。這五衰相是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、衣無垢染，有垢染現，他們的布比人類的絲綢還要細，身上的衣服本來沒有髒的，現在變髒，就是將死的前兆。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、鬘舊不萎，今乃萎悴， 天人有很多的花蔓在身上，舊是指過去，本來花很新鮮的，現在枯萎了，表示他將死了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、兩腋汗流，二個腋窩下開始流汗。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、身便臭穢，身體開始有臭穢了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、天及天子不樂本座，天王及天子本來有很高的座位，現在不歡喜坐在原來的座位。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、釋相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋相，解釋天人將死的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">時彼天子偃臥林間，所有婇女與餘天子共為遊戲。彼既見已，由此因緣，生大憂苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這時天子躺在樹林間，原來和他遊戲的美麗天女離他而去，跟其他的天子共同遊戲歡樂。看到這些景象，知道自己不能再享受這些欲樂，天福快要盡，已經要墮落了，內心很憂愁苦惱，悶悶不樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、陵懱苦3　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科陵懱苦，天人也有被人瞧不起的痛苦，分三科；第一科標，標出受陵懱苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復受陵懱悚慄之苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面是說將要死會有的受苦情況。現在是還沒有死，還存在時，要受其他更有福德的天子欺負瞧不起，內心恐怖顫慄的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，先問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這話怎麼說呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p301"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="57458:2975"></a>由有廣大福聚成就及廣大五欲天子生時，所餘薄福諸舊天子見已惶怖。由此因緣，受大憂苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　當有成就廣大福報很多的福聚集在一起、能受用廣大五欲的天子誕生時，原來福報比較小的天子看到有大福報大威德的天子心裏就張惶恐怖。由於這種因緣，受到很大的憂苦。因為再也不能受用那麼廣大的欲，這欲都被大福聚的天子拿去受用了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果這種人修得不夠，在人間有匱乏苦，到了天上還是有被陵懱苦，可能是被搶走了或是被輕視的痛苦，自己心裏也有憂苦，福報不夠就是這樣。人跟人之間也是有很大的差別，福報夠的人說話有力量，福報不夠的人說再多也是沒有用，所說的話人微言輕，人家就不相信，或者受用的情況就不同，天人也有這種痛苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、斫截等苦3　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科斫截等苦，被砍截肢苦，分三科；第一科標，標出受斫截等苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又受斫截破壞、驅擯殘害之苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又要受被砍傷截斷破壞肢節，被驅逐擯除出去，被兵器殘害的痛苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，先問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這種情況是怎麼樣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、釋2　酉一、斫截破壞苦2　戌一、辨相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科斫截破壞苦，受斫截破壞苦，又分二科；第一科辨相，說明斫截破壞苦的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由天與非天共戰諍時，天與非天互相違拒，即執四仗，所謂金、銀、頗胝、琉璃，共相戰鬥。爾時諸天及與非天，或斷支節，或破其身，或復致死。若傷身斷節，續還如故，若斷其首，即便殞歿。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於天人與阿修羅共相戰諍時，天人與阿修羅互相違逆抗拒，彼此拿著四種材料做的兵器互相打鬥，包括金、銀、頗胝（類似琉璃寶的材料，有的地方說是玻璃，應該不是玻璃，玻璃一打就碎了）及琉璃寶，互相戰鬥。那時諸天及阿修羅，有的被截斷支節，有破壞身體的，或因此而死的。如果傷害身體截斷肢節，會繼續補上恢復原狀，例如腳被砍斷，馬上就長出另外一隻腳，但是如果將頭砍斷，就真的死了。《摩訶般若波羅蜜經》說，當天人與阿修羅戰諍時，釋提桓因來問佛怎麼辦啊？佛要他誦：「摩訶般若波羅蜜」，就念這幾句話，阿修羅的兵器就通通掉下來，不能再跟諸天作戰了。「摩訶般若波羅蜜」，是大般若，是空，空的力量，使令阿修羅沒有力量來跟諸天作戰。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、料簡2　亥一、天與非天差別2　天一、總明彼苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科料簡，詳細的簡別，分二科；第一科天與非天差別，說明天與非天的差別，又分二科；第一科總明彼苦，總相說明天與非天的痛苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天與非天互有他勝，然天多勝，力勢彊故。然其彼二，若為他勝，即退入自宮，己之同類竟不慰問。由此因緣，便懷憂慼。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　天與阿修羅彼此都有被對方打勝的情況，但是多數是天勝利，阿修羅失敗，因為天的力量比較強。然而天與阿修羅雙方，如果被對方戰勝，就要退回自己住的宮殿，自己的同伴沒有人會慰問，沒有人關心。由於這種因緣，就心懷憂慼，悶悶不樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、別顯所為</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別顯所為，各別顯示天與非天的作為。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p302"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若天得勝，便入非天宮中，為悅其女，起此違諍；若非天得勝，即入天宮，為求四種酥陀味故，共相戰諍。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　他們為什麼打仗？這裏將原因說出來了。如果天人得勝，就到阿修羅的宮中，去跟阿修羅女歡悅，天人是為了討得阿修羅女，所以彼此互相違背互相鬥爭。如果阿修羅勝了，就跑到天宮中，求取青黃赤白四種酥陀美味，為此互相戰爭。這是說明彼此戰爭的原因，天人為了搶修羅女為妻，阿修羅是為了拿到青黃赤白四種天人的食物，而互相戰爭。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、非天亦天趣攝2　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科非天亦天趣攝，阿修羅也是屬於天趣所攝，分二科；第一科標，標出屬於天趣所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸非天，當知天趣所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又阿修羅，應當知道也是屬於天道眾生所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、釋2　地一、趣攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科趣攝，說出屬天趣所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">然由意志多懷詐幻，諂誑多故，不如諸天為淨法器。由此因緣，有時經中說為別趣，實是天類。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這種天界的阿修羅有天福沒有天德，為什麼沒有天德呢？因為他們內心大多不誠實，懷著詐欺、狡猾、虛偽，很多諂媚欺誑，內外不一致，有欺騙的行為語言，不如諸天的內心清淨善良。由於這些因緣，因此有時經中說阿修羅趣是別趣所攝，事實上是天趣所攝。一般說五趣，是指天、人、畜生、餓鬼、地獄。若說六道，則加阿修羅趣。又阿修羅一道，也可以廣攝在天、人、畜生、鬼趣四趣之中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、得名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科得名，結得名非天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由不受行諸天法故，說為非天。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為不受行諸天道德的法，沒有諸天善良的心，所以稱為非天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、驅擯苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科驅擯苦，受驅逐擯出之苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有彊力天子，纔一發憤，諸劣天子便被驅擯，出其自宮。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　天人也是一樣強欺弱。如果有彊力天子，只要一生氣，比較弱的天人就被驅逐擯出自己的宮殿。天人有這些種種的苦，做天也有天的苦，三界輪迴都是苦的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結受三種苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故諸天受三種苦。謂死墮苦，陵懱苦，斫截破壞、殘害驅擯苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此欲界天趣的有情受三種苦：一、死墮苦，五衰相現苦。二、陵懱苦，福報不夠的會被大福報的天人所欺負所輕視的苦。三、斫截破壞、殘害驅擯苦，與阿修羅打仗互相砍掉彼此的身體，被破壞、殘害、驅逐出去的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p303"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、色無色天2　午一、簡他苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科色無色天，說明色無色天無苦受，分二科；第一科簡他苦，簡別他們沒有其他趣眾生的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又色無色界有情無有如是等苦，由彼有情非苦受器故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又色、無色界的有情有禪定，所以沒有前面所說的這些苦，由於那裡的人沒有苦受的果報。已經有禪定，身體是喜樂的境界，初禪、二禪都有喜樂、三禪樂受、四禪捨受，無色界的有情也都是捨受相應，所以他們不是苦受器。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顯自苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯自苦，顯出有麤重苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">然由麤重苦故，說彼有苦。有煩惱故，有障礙故，於死及住不自在故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　然而由煩惱種子未斷的麤重苦，說他們有苦。有煩惱故，他們的煩惱是有覆無記性；有障礙故，能覆障聖道，雖然死時沒有解肢節苦，可是因為沒有出離三界，死了以後也可能墮到五道，所以說於死不自在；於生命住時，色界有情有中等的麤重，無色界有情有細麤重，因此也不自在。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有煩惱故等者：麤重差別略有二十。（如顯揚論十九卷三頁說）今說色無色界有情，隨應當知彼麤重苦。謂煩惱麤重、障礙麤重、死及住麤重。由此說彼有麤重苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《顯揚聖教論》說麤重差別有二十種，在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59，1946頁說到麤重有十八種。現在說色無色界的有情，隨其所應，應當知道他們的麤重苦。煩惱麤重指煩惱種子。在《顯揚聖教論》中名性煩惱麤重；障礙麤重有六種，包括煩惱、業、異熟、定障、蓋障及所知障麤重，其中上二界有無明、愛、見、慢等煩惱障、所知障麤重、蓋障中掉舉及定障麤重中屬於滅盡定這一分；死麤重，臨命終時諸根亂性稱為死麤重，上二界雖然沒有解肢節使諸根亂性，而由煩惱種子未斷，必須繼續受其他趣的苦，也名死麤重；住麤重，一期壽命還有煩惱麤重等稱為住麤重。因此說色界無色界有麤重苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、簡無漏</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科簡無漏，簡別無漏是指聖人的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又無漏界中，一切麤重諸苦永斷。是故唯此是勝義樂，當知所餘一切是苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又無漏界中，圓滿的無漏界如阿羅漢或佛，一切愛見煩惱麤重乃至所知障麤重諸苦永斷，這是勝義樂，應當知道其他一切有情都是苦。還沒有圓滿如初果等或初地等，仍有麤重苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無漏界中一切麤重諸苦永斷等者：通說三界二十種麤重差別，是名一切麤重。通說五趣諸受用苦，是名諸苦。無漏界中永斷此故，說唯有樂。當知此樂名為常樂，無漏界攝，離貪瞋癡方證得故。如下自說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/05.htm#3005:3292">陵本五卷五頁一行333</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　包括欲界、色界、無色界三界，有二十種麤重差別，稱為一切麤重。包括五趣種種受用的苦，稱為諸苦。無漏界中，已永遠斷除這些麤重，沒有這些苦，所以說只有樂。應當知道這種快樂是常樂，無漏界所攝，必須遠離貪瞋癡才能證得。如〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷5，134頁中還會解釋勝義樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p304"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、受用樂2　卯一、簡那落迦等2　辰一、舉四種那落迦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科受用樂，說明五趣有情受用樂的情況，分二科；第一科簡那落迦等，簡別地獄眾生沒有受用樂的情況，又分二科；第一科舉四種那落迦，舉出四種地獄。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="39507:3008"></a>又於四種那落迦中無有樂受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於前面說的四種地獄當中是沒有樂受的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又於四種那落迦中無有樂受者：謂如前說大那落迦、近邊那落迦、寒那落迦、獨一那落迦，是名四種那落迦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面說的大地獄有八種，近邊地獄有很多個，寒冰地獄也有八個，獨一地獄有很多個，加起來稱為四種地獄。四種地獄中的眾生完全沒有樂受。</span></span></span></div>
