<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、例三種餓鬼</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例三種餓鬼，前面說三種餓鬼也沒有樂受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如那落迦中，三種餓鬼中亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如地獄中的眾生完全沒有樂受，三種餓鬼中也一樣沒有樂受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、顯餘趣2　辰一、有苦雜</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯餘趣，顯示其他畜生、人、天等眾生有樂受，分二科；第一科有苦雜，樂受中有苦摻雜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸大力鬼、傍生、人中，有外門所生資具樂可得，然為眾苦之所相雜。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一種大力鬼是有財力的，畜生及人中有些外門所生資具樂可得，可是有眾多苦惱夾雜在其中。例如受用資具樂過多或過少所生苦，追求資具樂所生苦等。這是說到餘趣受樂有苦雜的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、無苦雜2　巳一、人趣輪王2　午一、總顯彼樂4　未一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無苦雜，說明有一種人受樂時沒有痛苦夾雜在裏面，分二科；第一科人趣輪王，人趣輪王所受樂，又分二科；第一科總顯彼樂，說明當轉輪聖王受的快樂，又分四科；第一科標，標出原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="1581:3015"></a>又人趣中，轉輪王樂最勝微妙。由彼輪王出現世時，有成就七寶自然出現，故說彼王具足七寶。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在人趣當中，轉輪聖王修很多如供養三寶等福報，他的樂是最殊勝最微妙的。因為輪王出現時，成就七寶自然出現，所以說轉輪聖王具足七寶。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，先問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為七？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪七種寶呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p305"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所謂輪寶、象寶、馬寶、末尼珠寶、女寶、主藏臣寶、主兵臣寶。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　包括輪寶、象寶、馬寶、末尼珠寶、女寶、主藏臣寶、主兵臣寶。輪寶是輪王的交通工具，當轉輪聖王出來時，海水下降，黃金的道路就出現。輪寶能在空中飛來飛去，也能夠在地上走，轉輪聖王想去那裏，輪寶就帶他到那裏去，因此稱為輪寶。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　輪寶有金銀銅鐵四種，分別為金、銀、銅、鐵四種輪王所乘。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　象寶，指白色六牙象，於晨朝時乘之周行四海，即時還宮。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　馬寶，指紺青色有象力之駿馬，能飛行，與象寶同為轉輪王之乘駕。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　末尼珠寶，指寶珠，有光明照王宮內。如果將寶珠在夜中置於高幢上，則光照一由旬，城中人民都起身作務，以為是天亮了。據說這是釋提桓因送輪王的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　女寶，輪王有一個很美麗的夫人，又名玉女寶，指美麗且具足德行之女。經中說她顏色從容，面貌端正，冬則身溫，夏則身涼，舉身毛孔發出旃檀香氣，口出優缽羅花香，言語柔軟，舉止安詳。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　主藏臣寶，有大臣為輪王所用，這些大臣知道大地那裡有寶藏，能取出供王使用。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　主兵臣寶，指智謀雄猛英略獨決的掌兵大將，所向無敵，戰無不勝，攻無不克。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、指</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科指，指出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">爾時輪寶等現，其相云何？七寶現相，如經廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這時有輪寶等顯現在世間，它的相狀如何？七寶現相，如經中廣說。可以參考《中阿含經》60經《王相應品．四洲經》或《雜阿含經》卷27、《增一阿含經》卷33《等法品經》、《輪王七寶經》、《菩薩瓔珞本業經》卷上〈賢聖學觀品〉等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋彼種類4　未一、王四洲者</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋彼種類，解釋輪王的種類，分四科；第一科王四洲者，統治東毗提訶洲、西瞿陀尼洲、北拘盧洲、南贍部洲這四大洲的金輪王。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼輪王王四洲者，一切小王望風順化，各自白言：某城邑聚落，天之所有，唯願大王垂恩教敕，我等皆當為天僕隸。爾時輪王便即敕令：汝等諸王！各於自境以理獎化，當以如法，勿以非法。又復汝等於國於家勿行非法行，勿行不平等行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是統治四洲的金輪王不用去打仗，一切小王由聽聞到輪王的道德就隨順輪王的教化，各自向金輪王說：我有某個城邑聚落，是天之所有，都歸大王所有，唯願大王能教導及慈悲愛護，我們都願意作天的奴僕，願意為您做事。這時轉輪聖王就下令：各位國王，你們應該在自己的國境以合道理的事來獎勵、勸化老百姓，應當如法推行十善法，不可以不如法。又你們對於國家和家庭不能造作不如法行，不要做不平等不合道理的行為。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、王三洲者</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科王三洲者，統治東、南、西三大洲的銀輪王，三洲就是除掉北拘盧洲以外。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼輪王王三洲者，先遣使往，然後從化。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若統治東、南、西三大三洲的銀輪王就差一點，必須要派遣使者到這些小國去，然後這些小國的國王才會順服他。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、王二洲者</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科王二洲者，只有統治東毗提訶洲、南贍部洲的銅輪王。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼輪王王二洲者，興師現威，後乃從化。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果是統治東毗提訶洲、南贍部洲二洲的銅輪王，必須發動軍隊，顯現他的威力，然後其他小國的國王才能臣服於他。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p306"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、王一洲者</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科王一洲者，是指統治南贍部洲的鐵輪王。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼輪王王一洲者，便自往彼，奮戈揮刃，然後從化。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最沒有威德力的是統治南贍部洲一洲的鐵輪王，必須親自到那些小國家去，拿起刀槍比劃比劃，現威之後才能服從他的教化。奮戈揮刃，本論沒有詳細解釋，而《俱舍論》說所有的輪王都不用殺死對方，威力不足時，還要在那裡比劃比劃，例如說現在有大炮多少，有火箭多少，展示一下自己的威力，然後對方才會服從教化。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、三界諸天3　午一、欲界2　未一、顯受樂2　申一、列種種2　酉一、正說諸天2　戌一、總說2　亥一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科三界諸天，諸天的樂沒有痛苦夾雜在裏面，分三科；第一科欲界，欲界諸天，又分二科；第一科顯受樂，顯示欲界諸天所受樂，又分二科；第一科列種種，列出種種的快樂，又分二科；第一科正說諸天，正說諸天所受樂，又分二科；第一科總說，總說諸天所受樂，又分二科；第一科標，先標出來受廣大天之富樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，諸天受其廣大天之富樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，欲界諸天受用廣大天的富足與快樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋2　天一、樂住本座</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科樂住本座，如果還沒死時是樂住本座。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">形色殊妙，多諸適悅，於自宮中而得久住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界諸天的天人的身形容色非常殊勝微妙，很多很如意的事，能夠在自己的天宮裏久住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、其身清潔2　地一、顯自</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科其身清潔，欲界諸天的身體很清潔，分二科；第一科顯自，顯示自身清潔無臭。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">其身內外皆悉清潔，無有臭穢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　他們身體內外都很清潔，沒有臭惡汙穢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、簡他</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡他，簡別人身內多有不淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又人身內多有不淨，所謂塵垢筋骨脾腎心肝；彼皆無有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　人為什麼很骯髒呢？因為人有灰塵、汙垢，還有筋骨、腎臟、脾臟、心臟、肝臟，而天人都沒有，他們的身體沒有內臟，業力使他們很清潔，沒有臭穢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、別辨2　亥一、依持相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別說明，分二科；第一科依持相，說明諸天宮殿的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p307"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼諸天有四種宮殿，所謂金、銀、頗胝、琉璃所成，種種文綵綺飾莊嚴。種種臺閣、種種樓觀、種種層級、種種窗牖、種種羅網，皆可愛樂。種種末尼以為綺鈿，周匝放光，共相照曜。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又欲界天人住在四種宮殿，由金、銀、頗胝、琉璃四種材料造成，宮殿內有種種美麗的文綵、圖畫、飾品、雕樑畫棟十分莊嚴。種種亭臺樓閣，種種樓殿之類的高大建築物，種種的階梯，種種的窗戶，種種的寶網，都非常可愛，看了令人愛樂。有種種的末尼珠做的花片裝飾牆面，天宮周圍內外都放出光明，共相照曜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、資具相2　天一、舉種類9　地一、食樹</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科資具相，諸天的資具相，分二科；第一科舉種類，舉出資具的種類，又分九科；第一科食樹，諸天的飲食由樹裏面出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有食樹，從其樹裏出四食味，名曰酥陀，所謂青黃赤白。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有食樹，天人的食品，天人的甘露，是長在樹上面，從樹裏面出產四種食品名為酥陀，有青黃赤白四種。這也是阿修羅與他們戰爭的原因，因為想要搶得這四種食物。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、飲樹</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科飲樹，飲料也是從樹裏面出來的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有飲樹，從此流出甘美之飲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有飲樹，從這種樹會流出很甘甜好喝的飲料。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、乘樹</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科乘樹，車子也是從樹裏面出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有乘樹，從此出生種種妙乘，所謂車輅輦輿等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有乘樹，是生出交通工具的樹，從這種樹可以變化出很多微妙的交通工具，所謂車子，輅也是一種車子，輦是轎子，輿是一種有蓋的車，這是用古代的話來形容，如果是現代可能就是有各種的汽車、飛機乃至火箭這些交通工具都有。天人的交通工具也是很優美很微妙的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地四、衣樹</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科衣樹，還有衣服的樹。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有衣樹，從此出生種種妙衣，其衣細軟，妙色鮮潔，雜綵間飾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有專門生出衣服的衣樹，從此衣樹生出種種微妙的衣服，這些衣服非常細緻柔軟，顏色十分美妙鮮麗清潔，有很多美麗的圖案裝飾在衣服上面。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地五、莊嚴具樹</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科莊嚴具樹，生出裝飾品的樹。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有莊嚴具樹，從此出生種種微妙莊嚴之具，所謂末尼、臂印、耳璫、環釧，及以手足綺飾之具。如是等類諸莊嚴具，皆以種種妙末尼寶而間飾之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　還有一種樹稱為莊嚴具樹，從這種樹能生出種種微妙莊嚴的飾品，如：末尼珠、臂環、臂印、耳墜子、手環及裝飾手、腳的綺麗美妙的飾品。這些莊嚴具，都以種種妙末尼寶而間錯裝飾，價值連城。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p308"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地六、熏香鬘樹</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科熏香鬘樹，生出熏香華鬘的樹。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有熏香鬘樹，從此出生種種塗香、種種熏香、種種華鬘。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有熏香鬘樹，從這種樹會生出種種的塗香、種種熏香及種種的華鬘，可以掛在頭上或脖子上。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地七、大集會樹</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科大集會樹，能供大集會的樹。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有大集會樹，最勝微妙。其根深固五十踰繕那，其身高挺百踰繕那，枝條及葉遍覆八十踰繕那；雜華開發，其香順風熏百踰繕那，逆風熏五十踰繕那。於此樹下，三十三天雨四月中，以天妙五欲共相娛樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有大集會樹，這是天人聚集在一起的地方，這種樹最殊勝微妙。它的根很深很堅固，有五十踰繕那，它的樹高挺拔達百踰繕那，枝條及樹葉遍滿覆蓋八十踰繕那那麼廣的範圍；這種樹開滿各式各樣的香花，花香順風能熏到百踰繕那遠的地方，逆風可以熏五十踰繕那。在這種樹下，欲界的第二天三十三天，在雨季的四個月當中，都在此處以天上的五欲來互相娛樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地八、歌笑舞樂之樹</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科歌笑舞樂之樹，提供歌笑舞樂之樹。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有歌笑舞樂之樹，從此出生歌笑舞等種種樂器。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有歌笑舞樂之樹，從這種樹能出生唱歌、歡笑、跳舞、音樂等種種樂器。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地九、資具樹</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科資具樹，提供資具之樹。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有資具之樹，從此出生種種資具，所謂食飲之具、坐臥之具，如是等類種種資具。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有資具樹，從這種樹能出生種種資具，包括飲食所需要的工具，還有床座，或椅子等各種生活所需的資具。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、明受用</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明受用，說到資具的受用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼諸天欲受用時，隨欲隨業，應其所須，來現手中。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這些欲界天的天人，想要受用諸欲時，隨他心裡的願望，隨他的業力，滿他的所願，出現在手上。天人欲的受用不是沒有限度的，由業力、福報大小，到他的手中，微妙的程度也不同，心裡一想，樹就來供應他各樣資具。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p309"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、兼顯非天等2　戌一、非天</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科兼顯非天等，將阿修羅等受用樂的情況也說一下，分二科；第一科非天，指阿修羅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸非天，隨其所應，受用種種宮殿富樂應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又諸非天，指阿修羅，也是隨其所欲、隨其所須，隨他的業力，也能受用種種的宮殿，富足快樂的情形也與天人一樣，因為他們也有天福。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又諸非天隨其所應受用種種宮殿富樂者：非天宮殿在蘇迷盧下，依水而居。如前意地已說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/02.htm#3067:1300">陵本二卷十一頁144</a>）彼亦天趣所攝，受用富樂，隨應當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿修羅的宮殿在蘇迷盧山下，依水而居。如前〈意地〉卷2，65頁中已經說過。阿修羅也是屬於天趣所攝，受用種種的富樂，隨其所相應的應當知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、北洲2　亥一、有勝受用2　天一、資具</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科北洲，說明北拘盧洲的人所受用樂，分二科；第一科有勝受用，有殊勝的受用，又分二科；第一科資具，受用的資具。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又北拘盧洲有如是相樹，名曰如意。彼諸人眾所欲資具，從樹而取。不由思惟，隨其所須，自然在手。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又北拘盧洲的人有一種樹，名為如意。那裏的人如果想要甚麼資具，也是從樹上取得。不用去想，隨他們需要甚麼，不需要動腦筋製造，自然就會有需要的資具出現在手中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、粳稻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科粳稻，受用的粳稻。</span></span></span></div>

<p><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有粳稻，不種而穫。無有我所。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有粳稻，他們的稻米不用去種，有地味自然會長出來就有收穫，而且不會據為我所有的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、無繫屬等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無繫屬等，北拘盧洲的人無繫屬。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼有情竟無繫屬、決定勝道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又那裏的人沒有繫屬，他們沒有父母，沒有奴婢僕使，想要什麼就有什麼，也不用人工去製造。他們是修十善業才到那裡去投生，在那裏也過著十善的生活，他們滿足現有的生活方式，沒有佛法，一切聖人絕對不會到那裡去，死了以後，來生會生天，有增上生，但沒有聖道的決定勝道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p310"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又彼有情竟無繫屬等者：無攝受事，名無繫屬。攝受有七，如前意地已說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/02.htm#3077:1530">陵本二卷十七頁165</a>）無念、正知、證煩惱斷，名無決定勝道。由是諸聖不更於彼受生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　他們沒有父母、妻子、奴婢、僕使、朋友、官僚、田宅邸市等攝受事，稱為無繫屬。攝受有七，如前〈意地〉卷2，72頁已經說過。他們沒有正念、正知，也不能斷煩惱，名為無決定勝道，只有增上生。因此聖人不會到那裏去。北拘盧洲是八難其中的一種難處，到那裏去不能修學佛法，因為生活太舒適了，想什麼就有什麼。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、顯殊勝3　酉一、依持相攝7　戌一、宮殿殊勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯殊勝，顯出殊勝處，分三科；第一科依持相攝，說明依報所攝殊勝相，又分七科；第一科宮殿殊勝，欲界天的宮殿很殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又天帝釋有普勝殿，於諸殿中最為殊勝。仍於其處有百樓觀，一一樓觀有百臺閣，一一臺閣有七房室，一一房室有七天女，一一天女有七侍女。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又天帝釋是釋提桓因，他有普勝殿，在所有宮殿中最為殊勝。在天帝的宮殿中有一百棟的高樓可以觀賞風景，每一個樓觀上面有一百座臺閣，每一個臺閣有七個房室，每一個房室有七個天女，每一個天女有七個侍女。百是形容很多，如果用一百來算就有四十九萬個侍女在那裡面，不過這是大約，就是上面很多高樓及蓋得很好的宮殿，宮殿很殊勝又很多，可以在那裡嬉戲遊樂。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、地界殊勝2　亥一、平正安樂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科地界殊勝，欲界天的土地也很殊勝，分二科；第一科平正安樂，平正安樂的殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼諸天所有地界，平正如掌，竟無高下。履觸之時，便生安樂，下足之時，陷便至膝，舉足之時，隨足還起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又彼諸天的地面是平正如掌，不會像人間高高低低，所以竟無高下。履，是指鞋子，鞋子踏到上面時就感覺很舒服很安樂，土很軟，軟到一踩下去就深陷至膝，腳舉起來的時後又恢復到原來的高度，又一樣是平正如掌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、新華遍布</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科新華遍布，新花遍布的殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於一切時，自然而有曼陀羅華遍布其上。時有微風吹去萎華，復引新者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於任何時辰，自然有曼陀羅花遍滿地上。經常有一陣陣微風吹來，將枯萎的花吹走，又吹來新的花，使新花遍布。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、街衢殊勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科街衢殊勝，街道的殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼天宮四面各有大街。其形殊妙，軌式可觀，清淨端嚴，度量齊整。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又天人的天宮四面都有大街，形狀很殊勝微妙，道路非常的整齊劃一美觀，路面很清潔而且很莊嚴，路開得很整齊，不過這不是用人工鋪設，是業所感得的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、宮門殊勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科宮門殊勝，宮門的殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p311"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復於四面有四大門，規模宏壯，色相希奇，觀之無厭，實為殊絕。多有異類妙色藥叉常所守護。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於四面有四個大門，規模非常宏大壯觀，顏色特別奇妙，百看不厭，實在很殊勝、絕妙。有很多不同種類長得很好看的藥叉常常在那裡守護著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌五、園苑殊勝2　亥一、標列四園</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科園苑殊勝，花園也很殊勝，分二科；第一科標列四園，標列出有四個花園。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復於四面有四園苑。一名繢車，二名麤澀，三名和雜，四名喜林。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於天宮四面有四座花園。一、名繢車，擺著各式各樣美麗的車子。二、名麤澀，擺戰爭的武器等。三、名和雜，是諸天在受用各種欲樂的地方。四、名喜林，是諸天遊戲時的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、環四勝地</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科環四勝地，這四個花園外面有四個殊勝的景色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">其四園外有四勝地，色相殊妙，形狀可觀，端嚴無比。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這四座花園外面有四個殊勝的地方，色相很殊妙，形狀很可觀，端正莊嚴無與倫比。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌六、會處殊勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科會處殊勝，諸天聚會處的殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">其宮東北隅，有天會處，名曰善法。諸天入中，思惟、稱量、觀察妙義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在這天宮的東北角，有諸天聚會的處所，稱為善法堂。諸天聚集在那裡，思惟、籌量、觀察佛法種種微妙的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌七、石相殊勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科石相殊勝，石相的殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">近此園側，有如意石，其色黃白，形質殊妙，其相可觀，嚴麗無比。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　靠近花園的側邊，有如意石，稱可天心，天人想要什麼就會出現什麼，顏色是黃或白的，形狀質地很殊勝美妙，外相美觀，非常的莊嚴美麗無與倫比。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、身相攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科身相攝，身相所攝的殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="8423:3098"></a>又彼天身自然光曜。闇相若現，乃知晝去夜分方來。便於天妙五欲遊戲之中，懶惰睡眠。異類之鳥不復和鳴，由此等相以表晝夜。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　那裏也有白天黑夜，不過不是用太陽來分別，是用他們身體的光明來分別。太陽在須彌山的一半，他們在須彌山之上，所以天上沒有太陽，但是他們的身體自然會有光明照耀，當身體的光明消失闇相出現的時候，才知道日間已經過去夜間已經來了。天人一天到晚都在五欲遊戲之中，到身體光明不現時，就懶惰睡眠了。各式各樣的鳥不會再叫了，用這種相貌來表示日間跟夜間。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="04p312"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、資具相攝2　戌一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科資具相攝，使用資具的殊勝相，分二科；第一科標，標出唯發喜樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="32223:3101"></a><a name="5156:3101"></a>又彼諸天眾妙五欲甚可愛樂，唯發喜樂。彼諸天眾恆為放逸之所持行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又在那裏受生的諸天，有各式各樣微妙的色聲香味觸五欲，女人很美，音樂很妙，食物很美味，都很可愛，使令他們歡喜、快樂。因此天人常常唱歌跳舞嬉戲放逸，生活在放逸中而不自覺。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出資具。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">常聞種種歌舞音樂鼓噪之聲，調戲言笑談謔等聲。常見種種可意之色。常齅種種微妙之香。恆嘗種種美好之味。恆觸種種天諸婇女最勝之觸。恆為是樂牽引其意，以度其時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　常常聽到各式各樣唱歌、跳舞、音樂、打鼓等鼓噪之聲，及互相調戲、談笑風生、互開玩笑等聲。常常看到很美麗令人滿意的色相，如花草、樹木、人等都是很美的。常常齅到種種微妙的香味，吃的東西都是天廚妙供，是最好的，吃了又不會生病。恆常接觸種種天女柔軟細滑的最勝之觸。恆常被快樂的境界牽引著意識，時間是這樣過的，整天都在放逸快樂當中。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無著菩薩的有一個弟弟名師子覺，本來要到兜率天內院親近彌勒菩薩，後來就是在外院玩得太快樂，忘了到兜率天內院。經典上還有一個故事說，有一個人兒子死了，他很難過，就去請問佛，佛陀告訴他：唉呀！你不要難過了，你放下吧！你兒子早就不知道你是他的父親了，因為他現在已經在三十三天享樂，已經生天了。他不相信，佛就說：那我帶你去看。用神通帶他去看。看到兒子跟天女在那裏唱歌跳舞歡笑玩樂。這個父親就對他兒子說，孩子孩子啊！你還記不記得我啊！那孩子理都不理，你是誰？趕快走開，好臭喔！立刻將他趕走，然後他就啊！一聲，終於放下。因此下來以後就專心修學佛法，也出家修行，不再想他的孩子了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、簡無苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡無苦，簡別欲界天人沒有苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼諸天多受如是眾妙欲樂，常無疾病，亦無衰老，無飲食等匱乏所作俱生之苦，無如前說於人趣中有餘匱乏之苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又欲界諸天多分受用如上所說種種微妙欲樂，不會生病，也不會老化，也沒有飲食不夠等種種的俱生匱乏苦，也沒有在人趣當中其餘六種匱乏的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第四</span></strong></span></span><br />
&nbsp;</p>
